	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of countries and dependencies by population</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Countries and dependent territories by population</div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Countries_and_Dependencies_by_Population_in_2014.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Countries_and_Dependencies_by_Population_in_2014.svg/300px-Countries_and_Dependencies_by_Population_in_2014.svg.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="138" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Countries_and_Dependencies_by_Population_in_2014.svg/450px-Countries_and_Dependencies_by_Population_in_2014.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Countries_and_Dependencies_by_Population_in_2014.svg/600px-Countries_and_Dependencies_by_Population_in_2014.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="863" data-file-height="396" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Countries_and_Dependencies_by_Population_in_2014.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A map of world population in 2014</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:World_population_percentage.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/World_population_percentage.png/220px-World_population_percentage.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="238" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/World_population_percentage.png/330px-World_population_percentage.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/World_population_percentage.png/440px-World_population_percentage.png 2x" data-file-width="2006" data-file-height="2174" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:World_population_percentage.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>World population percentage by country as of 2017</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:World_Population_Cartogram_Map_2002.tif" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7d/World_Population_Cartogram_Map_2002.tif/lossless-page1-220px-World_Population_Cartogram_Map_2002.tif.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7d/World_Population_Cartogram_Map_2002.tif/lossless-page1-330px-World_Population_Cartogram_Map_2002.tif.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7d/World_Population_Cartogram_Map_2002.tif/lossless-page1-440px-World_Population_Cartogram_Map_2002.tif.png 2x" data-file-width="2362" data-file-height="1181" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:World_Population_Cartogram_Map_2002.tif" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A <a href="/wiki/Cartogram" title="Cartogram">cartogram</a> of the world population in 2002</div></div></div>
<p>This is a <b>list of <a href="/wiki/Country" title="Country">countries</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dependent_territory" title="Dependent territory">dependent territories</a> by <a href="/wiki/Population" title="Population">population</a></b>. It includes <a href="/wiki/List_of_sovereign_states" title="List of sovereign states">sovereign states</a>, inhabited <a href="/wiki/Dependent_territory" title="Dependent territory">dependent territories</a> and, in some cases, constituent countries of sovereign states, with inclusion within the list being primarily based on the ISO standard <a href="/wiki/ISO_3166-1" title="ISO 3166-1">ISO 3166-1</a>. For instance, the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> is considered as a single entity, while the constituent countries of the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">Kingdom of the Netherlands</a> are considered separately. In addition, this list includes certain <a href="/wiki/List_of_states_with_limited_recognition" title="List of states with limited recognition">states with limited recognition</a> not found in ISO 3166-1.
</p><p>Also given in percent is each country's population compared with the <a href="/wiki/World_population" title="World population">population of the world</a>, which the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> estimates at 7.74 billion as of today.
</p>
<div id="toc" class="toc"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Method">Method</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Method">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population_density" title="List of countries and dependencies by population density">List of countries and dependencies by population density</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_regional_organizations_by_population" title="List of regional organizations by population">List of regional organizations by population</a></div>
<p>Figures used in this chart are based on the most up to date <a href="/wiki/Population_projection" title="Population projection">estimate or projections</a><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> by the national <a href="/wiki/Census" title="Census">census</a> authority where available, and are usually rounded off. 
</p><p>Where updated national data are not available, figures are based on the projections for 2019 by the Population Division of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Department_of_Economic_and_Social_Affairs" title="United Nations Department of Economic and Social Affairs">United Nations Department of Economic and Social Affairs</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-unpop_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-unpop-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Because the compiled figures are not collected at the same time in every country, or at the same level of <a href="/wiki/Statistics" title="Statistics">accuracy</a>, the resulting numerical comparisons may create misleading conclusions. Furthermore, the addition of figures from all countries may not equal the world total.
</p><p>Areas that form integral parts of sovereign states, such as the <a href="/wiki/Countries_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Countries of the United Kingdom">countries of the United Kingdom</a>, are counted as part of the sovereign states concerned. Not included are other entities, such as the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;Note 1&#93;</a></sup> that are not sovereign states, and independent territories that do not have permanent populations, such as <a href="/wiki/Territorial_claims_in_Antarctica" title="Territorial claims in Antarctica">various countries' claims</a> to <a href="/wiki/Antarctica" title="Antarctica">Antarctica</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sovereign_states_and_dependencies_by_population">Sovereign states and dependencies by population</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Sovereign states and dependencies by population">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Note: All dependent territories or constituent countries that are parts of sovereign states are shown in <i>italics</i> and not assigned a numbered rank. In addition, sovereign states with limited recognition are not assigned a number rank.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Intercontinental">Intercontinental</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Intercontinental">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 25em; -webkit-column-width: 25em; column-width: 25em;">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
<div class="mw-references-wrap mw-references-columns"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-3">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The European Union is a <i><a href="/wiki/Sui_generis" title="Sui generis">sui generis</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Supranational_union" title="Supranational union">supranational union</a> whose sovereign members delegate to it by treaty certain powers that are often exercised by sovereign states. Its combined population has been estimated at 512,379,225 on January 1, 2018, and it would be ranked 3rd if it were included in the list. It has 6.62% of the world's population&#160; see <cite class="citation web"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" </li>
<li id="cite_note-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-4">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The census figure refers to <a href="/wiki/Mainland_China" title="Mainland China">mainland China</a>, excluding its <a href="/wiki/Special_administrative_regions_of_China" title="Special administrative regions of China">special administrative regions</a> of <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> and <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a>, the former of which returned to Chinese sovereignty on 1&#160;July 1997 and the latter on 20&#160;December 1999.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-5"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-5">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Does not include the figures of <a href="/wiki/Lakshadweep" title="Lakshadweep">Lakshadweep</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andaman_and_Nicobar_Islands" title="Andaman and Nicobar Islands">Andaman and Nicobar Islands</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-6"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-6">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Population of the <a href="/wiki/List_of_states_and_territories_of_the_United_States" title="List of states and territories of the United States">50 states</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">District of Columbia</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-7"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-7">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Including the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Crimea" title="Republic of Crimea">Republic of Crimea</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sevastopol" title="Sevastopol">Sevastopol</a>, Russia's disputed administrative areas on the <a href="/wiki/Crimea" title="Crimea">Crimean Peninsula</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukrainian</a> government and most of the world's other states consider the Crimean Peninsula <i><a href="/wiki/De_jure" title="De jure">de jure</a></i> a part of Ukraine's territory.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-8"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-8">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Population of the 18 <a href="/wiki/Regions_of_France" title="Regions of France">regions of France</a>. Excluding Overseas Territories and Collectivities: <a href="/wiki/French_Polynesia" title="French Polynesia">French Polynesia</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Caledonia" title="New Caledonia">New Caledonia</a>, <a href="/wiki/French_Southern_and_Antarctic_Lands" title="French Southern and Antarctic Lands">French Southern and Antarctic Lands</a>, <a href="/wiki/Clipperton_Island" title="Clipperton Island">Clipperton Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saint_Barth%C3%A9lemy" title="Saint Barthlemy">Saint Barthlemy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Collectivity_of_Saint_Martin" title="Collectivity of Saint Martin">Saint Martin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saint_Pierre_and_Miquelon" title="Saint Pierre and Miquelon">Saint Pierre and Miquelon</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wallis_and_Futuna" title="Wallis and Futuna">Wallis and Futuna</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-9"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-9">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excluding the 14 <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories" title="British Overseas Territories">Overseas Territories</a> and 3 <a href="/wiki/Crown_dependencies" title="Crown dependencies">Crown dependencies</a> shown separately.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-10"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-10">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Including <a href="/wiki/Zanzibar" title="Zanzibar">Zanzibar</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-11"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-11">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excluding the <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_Republic_of_Crimea" title="Autonomous Republic of Crimea">Autonomous Republic of Crimea</a> and City of <a href="/wiki/Sevastopol" title="Sevastopol">Sevastopol</a>, Ukraine's administrative areas on the <a href="/wiki/Crimea" title="Crimea">Crimean Peninsula</a> which are disputed with and <i>de facto</i> administered by Russia. However includes all territory in the <a href="/wiki/Donbass" title="Donbass">Donbass</a> region where there are ongoing insurgencies by separatist forces.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-12"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-12">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excluding the population of the <a href="/wiki/Territorial_dispute" title="Territorial dispute">disputed territory</a> of <a href="/wiki/Western_Sahara" title="Western Sahara">Western Sahara</a> (<a href="/wiki/Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic</a>).</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-13"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-13">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a> (Republic of China) also includes the minor islands of <a href="/wiki/Kinmen" title="Kinmen">Kinmen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Matsu_Islands" title="Matsu Islands">Matsu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Penghu" title="Penghu">Penghu</a>, etc. The UN <a href="/wiki/China_and_the_United_Nations" title="China and the United Nations">does not recognize</a> the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="Republic of China">Republic of China</a> (<a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>) as a <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">sovereign state</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-14"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-14">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Includes <a href="/wiki/Somaliland" title="Somaliland">Somaliland</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-15"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-15">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excludes <a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-16"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-16">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excludes <a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Abkhazia</a> (242,862, census 2011) and <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a> (53,559, census 2015).</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-17"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-17">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excludes <a href="/wiki/Transnistria" title="Transnistria">Transnistria</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-18"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-18">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Kosovo is the subject of a territorial dispute between the <a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Republic of Kosovo</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Republic of Serbia</a>. The Republic of Kosovo <a href="/wiki/2008_Kosovo_declaration_of_independence" title="2008 Kosovo declaration of independence">unilaterally declared independence</a> on 17 February 2008, but <a href="/wiki/Kosovo%E2%80%93Serbia_relations" title="KosovoSerbia relations">Serbia continues to claim</a> it as part of its <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_Province_of_Kosovo_and_Metohija" title="Autonomous Province of Kosovo and Metohija">own sovereign territory</a>. The two governments <a href="/wiki/Belgrade%E2%80%93Pristina_negotiations" title="BelgradePristina negotiations">began to normalise relations</a> in 2013, as part of the <a href="/wiki/Brussels_Agreement_(2013)" title="Brussels Agreement (2013)">2013 Brussels Agreement</a>. Kosovo has been recognized as an independent state by <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Kosovo" title="International recognition of Kosovo">112</a> out of 193 <a href="/wiki/Member_states_of_the_United_Nations" title="Member states of the United Nations">United Nations member states</a>, while <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Kosovo" title="International recognition of Kosovo">12</a> states have recognized Kosovo only to later withdraw their recognition.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-19"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-19">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Administration is split between <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic</a>, both of which claim the entire territory.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-20"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-20">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>De facto</i> independent, <i>de jure</i> part of <a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Moldova</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-21"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-21">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>De facto</i> independent, <i>de jure</i> part of <a href="/wiki/Cyprus" title="Cyprus">Cyprus</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-22"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-22">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Abkhazia</a> is the subject of a territorial dispute between the <a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Republic of Abkhazia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a>. The Republic of Abkhazia unilaterally declared independence on 23 July 1992, but Georgia continues to claim it as part of its <a href="/wiki/Government_of_the_Autonomous_Republic_of_Abkhazia" title="Government of the Autonomous Republic of Abkhazia">own sovereign territory</a>. Abkhazia has received formal recognition as an independent state from <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Abkhazia_and_South_Ossetia" title="International recognition of Abkhazia and South Ossetia">7</a> out of 193 <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> <a href="/wiki/Member_states_of_the_United_Nations" title="Member states of the United Nations">member states</a>, 2 of which have subsequently withdrawn their recognition.
</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-23"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-23">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>De facto</i> independent, <i>de jure</i> part of <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan" title="Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-24"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-24">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a>'s status is disputed. It  considers itself to be an independent state, but this is recognised by <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Abkhazia_and_South_Ossetia#States_formally_recognising_Abkhazia_or_South_Ossetia_as_independent" title="International recognition of Abkhazia and South Ossetia">only a  few other countries</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgian</a> government and most of the  world's other states consider South Ossetia <i><a href="/wiki/De_jure" title="De jure">de jure</a></i>  a part of Georgia's territory.
</span>
</li>
</ol></div></div>
